I told her that she just needed to deduct the deposit, but I didn't really want to sign it. She kept chasing me from the first floor to the sixth floor to ask me to sign it. When she saw that I didn't sign it, she went to ask my wife to sign it, which made things very unpleasant. Which hotel would chase people from the first floor to the sixth floor for a few dozen dollars, and follow them all the way to the door of the room? If the waiter asked me to sign directly, I would have signed it. Why did she ask me to pay it myself? I don't understand. Is this what a five-star hotel does? She chased guests from the first floor to the sixth floor. I told her that she just needed to deduct the deposit, but she still wouldn't give in. She doesn't feel ashamed, but I do.
